 iske alaava rigerv bank ne is faisle ke liye vaishvik str par teji se badalte kaarobaari maahaul kaa bhi hawala diya he

 The meeting consists of 3 members from the Reserve Bank and 3 experts in financial matters
 samiksha kii adhyakshata khud rigerv bank governor karte hai
 What is the repo rate: The rate of interest at which the Reserve Bank gives loans to other banks in the country is called repo rate
 bainkon ke liye yah rate apane graahakon ko lone kaa byaaj tay karne ke kaam aata he
 Whenever a reduction in the repo rate is announced in a monetary policy, it simply means that now your banks will make all your loans cheaper
 masalan, home lone, vehical lone ityadi kam daron par muhaiyaa honge
 What is the reverse repo rate? All banks have to deposit all the cash collected above a certain cash in the Reserve Chest's currency chest
 rigerv bank is reverse repo rate par jamaaye karaae gaye cash par bainko ko byaaj detaa he
 Through this, the Reserve Bank decides the availability of currency in the market
 kya he siaraar (nakad arakshit anupaat)rigerv bank ke niyam ke mutabik sabhi bainkon ko apni kul nakadi kaa ek nishchit hissaa rigerv bank ke paas rakhana hota he
 This fixed portion is called Cash Reserve Ratio (CRR)

 How is the election of a pope The process of electing a pope in Vatican City is very complicated
 duniyabar se chune gaye cardinals ko vatical city bulaayaa jaataa he
 The rule is that all of them should be below 80 years of age
 is baar 48 deshon ke 115 cardinal agle pope kaa chunaav karne jute hai
 Five of which arrived from India
 pope chunane kii puri kavayad aath charnon main puri hoti he
 First of all the cardinals gather in the chapel
 uske baad chapel ke ek kamare main shuru hota he agle pope ke liye chunavi marathon
 Three groups of three cardinals are formed, on which different work takes place
 pehla group ballat paper kii ginati karata he
 The second group counts again while the third group is assigned the responsibility of collecting the ballot after voting from the cardinals
 iske baad shuru hota he voting kaa kaam
 Each cardinal takes an oath and writes the name of his choice on the ballot and then puts it on a plate
 cardinalon kii pehali team kaa ek member ye tay karata he ki saare voter apana vot daal den
 After this, the second member gives the name of the ballot to the other member
 doosraa member bhi yahi kaam karke tisare member ko detaa he

 " chunaavon ke liye sarkari funding nahin hone ke chalate gaiyrkanoonee nakadi hi rajnatik dalon ke kaam aati he, jo ve pratyaashiyon or samarthak vyapaariyon se ekatra karti hai, or phir vahi nakadi reliyon ke aayojan, helicopteron ke intazaam or vot paane kii khatir 'tohfe' baantne main kharch kii jaati he
 The sudden demonetization announcement made by Prime Minister Narendra Modi last week has so far been praised by most voters who are troubled by corruption, but economists and a section of the population have also come to different views on the fairness and effectiveness of the move
 
 is kadam ke baad se bainkon or atm ke saamne lageen lambii-lambii linon ko lekar sabhi vipakshi dal ekajute hokar sarkaar par hamalaa bol rahe hai
 He also alleged in Parliament on Wednesday that big businessmen and some BJP officials had already been informed of the demonetisation decision, although the government forcefully denied the allegation and termed it as baseless
 uttar pradesh kii mukhyamantri rah chukin taqatvar netaa or basapa pramukh mayawati kaa kahana he ki notebandi kaa samay puri tarah rajnatik lagata he
 For many decades, other parties have been accusing Mayawati of collecting black money for her funding by taking money from candidates in exchange for party tickets
 ek varisht adhikari tathaa mayawati ke kareebi ne samachar agency roitre ko bataaya ki unki party kii kuch reliyaan radd kar di jaaengi, or uske sthaan par ghar-ghar jaakar prachaar zyaada kiya jayega
 The official said, "last month, we had to bring 300,000 villagers from all over UP to Lucknow for a day
 
 
 or sirf ham nahin, vot jeetne ke liye har party nichle str par isi tarah paisa kharch karti he
 
 
 " is vakt rajya main sattashin samaajawaadee party ke mathura ke netaa ashok agarwal ne kaha ki unhen votaron se sampark karne ke liye ab 1,000 walantiaron kii apni team par nirbhar rahanaa padegaa
 According to Reuters, activists from different parties in the city have reported that political parties are paying workers to stand in long lines to replace old notes in banks with new ones, so that tax inspectors New notes can be collected without being noticed
 in dinon ve event manager bhi chintit dikh rahe hai, jinka kaamkaaj aamtaur par chunaav ke dinon main kaaphi faltaa-phulataa he
 Rajesh Pratap, who has been in the business of arranging security for loud speakers, outdoor air conditioners and rallies for the last 10 years, says, "no political party other than BJP wants to hold a big rally before January
 
 
 sabhi partiyaan nakadi par nirbhar hai
 
 
 "comments haalanki pradhanmantri narendra modi ne vimudrikaran yaa notebandi ke faisle ko sidhe-sidhe chunavi funding ko 'saaf' karne se nahin joda he, lekin roitre ke mutabik, bijepi ke hi kuch padaadhikariyon (jinke naam roitre ne nahin bataae) ne kaha he ki pratidwandviyon ko isi saal isse pehle piem dwaara di gai chetavaniyon ko sunanaa chahie tha ki vah 'kaale dhan' par shikanja kasne ke prati gambhir hai
 According to CMS estimates, the parties spent a record Rs 37,000 crore in the 2014 elections
 partiyaan lambey samay se niyamon se bachane or nakadi ke bina kaam chalaane ke raste khoj chuki thim - reliyon ke liye sidhe 'daan dene waalon' se hi bhugtan karvaa diya jaataa tha, yaa votaron ko rijhaane ke liye mobile phone richarge jaise 'tohfon' kaa kharch sthaneey vyapaaree kar diya karte the
 Pradeep Mathur's remarks indicate that the BJP is more capable of dealing with this cash crisis than its rivals and allegedly having close ties to large corporate 'donors', thereby winning it in Uttar Pradesh
 Will help, and this victory of UP is very important in Prime Minister Narendra Modi's plan to win the 2019 Lok Sabha elections
 It holds
 prachaar abhiyaanon kii funding par nazar rakhane vaale dilli sthit centre for media studies (siemes) ke mutabik, uttar pradesh jaise rajya main kul funding ke do-tihaai se bhi kam ke liye bijepi nakadi par nirbhar he, jabaki mana jaataa he ki samaajawaadee party (sapa) or bahujan samaaj party (basapa) jaise kshetreey dal apane prachaar par hone vaale kul kharch ke 80 se 95 pratishat hisse ke liye nakadi par nirbhar karte hai
 Milan Vaishnav, a South Asia expert at the Washington-based Carnegie Endowment for International Peace, said, "there is an assessment that it will hurt everyone, but if comparatively, the BJP will be able to come out of it more strongly
" 
 
 " With no government funding for elections, the illegal cash is used by political parties, which they collect from candidates and pro-businessmen, and then the same cash for organizing rallies, arranging helicopters and distributing 'gifts' to get votes
 Is spent in pichley hafte pradhanmantri narendra modi dwaara achaanak kii gai vimudrikaran kii ghoshnaa ko ab tak bhrashtachar se pareshaan rahe zyaadaatar votaron dwaara saraahaa gaya he, lekin arthshaastriyon tathaa aabaadi ke ek hisse main is kadam kii nishpakshta or prabhaav ko lekar alag-alag mat bhi saamne aae hai
 After this step, all opposition parties are attacking the government on the long lines in front of banks and atms
 unhone buudhvaar ko sansad main aarope bhi lagaaya ki bade vyapaariyon tathaa bijepi ke kuch padaadhikariyon ko pehle hi notebandi ke faisle kii jaankaree de di gai thi, haalanki sarkaar ne zordaar tareeke se is aarope kaa khandan karte hue ise aadharahin bataaya he
 Mayawati, the powerful leader and BSP chief who has been the Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh, says that the time of demonetisation seems completely political
 kai dashak se anya partiyaan mayawati par party tikat ke badale pratyaashiyon se paisa lekar apni funding ke liye kaala dhan jamaa karne kaa aarope lagaati ai hai
 a senior official and close to Mayawati told the news agency Reuters that some of her party's rallies would be canceled, and instead of going door-to-door campaigning would be done
 adhikari ne kaha, "pichley maheene hamen puure upi se 300,000 graminon ko ek din ke liye lakhanu laana padaa tha
 
 
 And not just us, every party spends the same amount of money to win votes
 
 
 " At this time Ashok Aggarwal, the leader of the ruling Samajwadi Party's Mathura state, said that he would now have to depend on his team of 1,000 volunteers to contact the voters
 roitre ke anusaar, shahar main alag-alag partiyon ke kaaryakartaaon ne bataaya he ki rajnatik dal kaaryakartaaon ko bainkon main puraane noton ko nae noton se badalawaane ke liye lagi lambii-lambii linon main khadey rahane ke liye paise de rahi hai, taaki tex inspectoron kii nazaron main aae bina nae note jutaaye ja saken
 These days the event managers are also looking worried, whose work usually flourishes during election days
 pichley 10 saal se laud spikaron, outdoor airkandishanron tathaa reliyon main suraksha kii vyavastha karne ke kaarobaar main lage rajesh pratap kaa kahana he, "bijepi ke alaava koi bhi rajnatik dal janvari se pehle badi raily yojit nahin karnaa chahta
 
 
 All parties are cash dependent
 
 
 "tippaniyan Although Prime Minister Narendra Modi's decision to demonetize or demonetize has not directly linked to 'clean' election funding, but according to Reuters, some BJP officials (whose names were not mentioned by Reuters) have said that rivals Earlier this year one should have heard the warnings given by the PM that he is serious about clamping down on 'black money'
 siemes ke anumaan ke anusaar, varsh 2014 ke chunaav main partiyon ne record 37,000 karod rupee kharch kiye the
 Parties had long found ways to evade the rules and run without cash - payments were made directly to 'donors' for rallies, or 'gifts' such as mobile phone recharges to woo voters
 Local merchants used to pay taxes
